NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE

[Part VI—Sec. 4

PUBLIC NOTICES
I, V. Vinod, natural son of (late) Thiru T. Vijayan, residing at No. 7, Sabhi Nagar, First Street, Ambattur Taluk,
Chennai-600 055, by way of Public Notice, I Inform that (late) S. George is my Step Father. My Step Father (late) S. George
passed away on 16th December 2016. Hereafter, I shall be known as G. VINOD.
Chennai,
12th April 2017.

V. VINOD,
(Step son)

S. Arunvinoth a male child born to V. Sekar on 17th April 1991 residing at No. 7/7, Mariyammankoil Street,
Koundampalayam, Coimbatore-641 030, has been living as a Transgender after an elaborate sexual reassignment
surgery by Dr. S. Natarajan., M.S (Gen.) Medical Panel, Coimbatore Medical College and Hospital, Coimbatore-641 018.
By this I, may be treated as a Transgender and shall henceforth be known as S ANUSHYA.
Coimbatore,
13th April 2017.

S. ARUNVINOTH

K. Gandhi, a male child born to Thiru M. Krishnan on 4th June 1994 residing at No. 51, Gajapathilal Street, Rajaji
Nagar, Triplicane, Chennai-600 005, has been living as a female after an elaborate sexual reassignment surgery at
Rajiv Gandhi General Government Hospital, Chennai-600 003. By this I, may be treated as a female and shall henceforth
be known as K. NABISHA.
Chennai,
13th April 2017.

K. GANDHI

R. Ranjithkumar, a male child born to Thiru R. Robert on 15th November 1994 residing at Nelam Basha Dharga,
Triplicane, Chennai-600 005 has been living as a female after an elaborate sexual reassignment surgery by
Dr. Shivam Vishwa Multi Speciality Hospital, Bengaluru. By this I, may be treated as a female and shall henceforth known
as R. VAISHNAVI.
Chennai,
13th April 2017.

R. RANJITHKUMAR
